***farrow.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:farrow.html>farrow</a> (54539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*farwe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*farȝe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*farh</i> (found only in the plural <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">faren</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fearh</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*farhaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">var</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">male pig; boar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:farah.html>farah</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pórḱos</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Irish">Middle Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mga">orc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">piglet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">porcus</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*porsę</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pig, piglet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">par̃šas</i>, Kurdish <i>purs</i>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*perḱ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:farrow.html>farrow</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">farrows</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A litter of piglets.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1949</b>,  Joseph Campbell,  <cite>The Hero with a Thousand <a href = vnd.unilang:faces.html>Faces</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">She <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the womb and the tomb: the sow that eats her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:farrow.html>farrow</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:farrow.html>farrow</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">farrows</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">farrowing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">farrowed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To give birth to a (litter of piglets).</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">farrowing</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:farrow.html>farrow</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of cows</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Not pregnant; not producing young (not calving) in a given season or year; barren.</li></ol>
</body>

***fata.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fata.html>fata</a> (47448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href = vnd.unilang:fata.html>fata</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fatōną</i>, from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ped-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to walk, stumble, fall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nn">fatta</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> through <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaten.html>vaten</a></i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vatten.html>vatten</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">fassen</i><span class="serial-comma">,</span> and to a certain degree <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fetch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nn"><a href = vnd.unilang:fata.html>fata</a></strong> (<i>present tense</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn">fatar</b>, <i>past tense</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:fata.html>fata</a></strong></b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:fata.html>fata</a></strong></b>, <i>passive infinitive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn">fatast</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn">fatande</b>, <i>imperative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn">fat</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take, <a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a>, seize
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1875</b>,  Elias <a href = vnd.unilang:blix.html>Blix</a>,  “Jesu, du <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> den Himmelveg”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nokre_Salmar" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nokre Salmar">Nokre Salmar</a></cite>  | <cite>Some hymns</cite> |  | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://urn.nb.no/URN:NBN:no-nb_digibok_2014101008123">[1]</a></sup>, Booklet III, Christiania |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Det_Norske_Samlaget" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Det Norske Samlaget">Samlaget</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://urn.nb.no/URN:NBN:no-nb_digibok_2014101008123?page=8">page 26</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nn">Ljoset <a href = vnd.unilang:det.html>det</a> inn i Myrkret skin // Myrkret <a href = vnd.unilang:det.html>det</a> inkje <a href = vnd.unilang:vil.html>vil</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fata.html>fata</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Light, it <a href = vnd.unilang:shines.html>shines</a> into the darkness. Darkness will not grasp it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to understand, comprehend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ignite <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to commence burning</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">fatal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fātālis</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>fatal (causing death or destruction)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fatso.html>fatso</a> (42338)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fatso.html>fatso</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fatsos</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fatsoes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> overweight.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fatwa.html>fatwa</a> (61101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">فَتْوَى</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fatwā</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">formal legal opinion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the verbal noun of <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">أَفْتَى</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ʾaftā</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to deliver a formal opinion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">مُفْتٍ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muftin</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><span class="Latn" lang="en">mufti</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the active participle of the same verb.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fatwa.html>fatwa</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fatwas</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fatawa</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Islam</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A legal opinion, decree or ruling issued by a mufti or other Islamic lawyer.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I think the <b>fatwas</b> on that website are totally unreliable.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fatwa.html>fatwa</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">fatwas</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">fatwaing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">fatwaed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To make somebody the subject of a <a href = vnd.unilang:fatwa.html>fatwa</a>, especially a ban or death sentence.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2000</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:anne.html>Anne</a> Weaver,  <cite>A Portrait of Egypt</cite>, page 141:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Unlike many writers and artists, Chahine <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> not <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <b>fatwaed</b> by the militants, but he felt threatened nevertheless.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:faun.html>faun</a> (47447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Faunus</i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Roman mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A woodland creature with pointed ears, <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a>, and short horns of a goat and a fondness for unrestrained revelry.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">entomology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of various nymphalid butterflies of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Faunis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Faunis"><i>Faunis</i></a></span>.</li></ol>

***faxen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:faxen.html>faxen</a> (13200)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">fax</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:faxen.html>faxen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fax (send a fax)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:recept.html>recept</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:faxen.html>faxen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I will <b>fax</b> the recipe to you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">doorfaxen</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fay.html>fay</a> (12622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">feyen</i>, <i class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fōgijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fōgō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">joint, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*paḱ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fasten, place</span><span Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">fōgia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">fōgian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to join</span><span More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">fang</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fay.html>fay</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">fays</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">faying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fayed.html>fayed</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To fit.</li>
<li>To join or unite closely or tightly.
<ul><li><i>Model Shipbuilders</i>, 2010:
<dl><dd>I have a strip cutter and I can cut the exact widths I need to fit, they are easy to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fay.html>fay</a></b> together and attach very firmly to the bulkheads.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>To lie close together.</li>
<li>To fadge.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to join or unite closely</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">affix</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">attach</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">put together</span>; see also Thesaurus:join</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">faying surface</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fay.html>fay</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:fay.html>fay</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:fay.html>fay</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Fitted closely together.
<ul><li>US Patent Application 20070033853, 2006:
<dl><dd>Under the four outer <a href = vnd.unilang:corners.html>corners</a> of the horizontal frame platform 22 are four tubular <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a> sleeves 23 that are <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fay.html>fay</a></b> together one at each outer corner.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fegien</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fæien</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cleanse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">fægja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cleanse, polish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fēgijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to decorate, make beautiful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pōḱ-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pēḱ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to clean, adorn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">feja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sweep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">feje</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sweep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">fegen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cleanse, scour, sweep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vegen.html>vegen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sweep, strike</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">feague</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fake</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fair</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fay.html>fay</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">fays</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">faying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fayed.html>fayed</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cleanse; clean out.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">faie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">fei</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a place or person possessed with magical properties</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">feie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">fee</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fairy", "<a href = vnd.unilang:fae.html>fae</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fairy</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>A fairy.

<dl><dd>that mighty Princesse <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> complaine / Of grieuous mischiefes, which a wicked <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fay.html>Fay</a></b> / <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>Had</a> wrought [...].</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fazant.html>fazant</a> (23183)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">faisant</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">fasaen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">fesant</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">phāsiānus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">φᾱσιανός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phāsianós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fazant.html>fazant</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fazanten.html>fazanten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fazant.html>fazantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pheasant, bird of the family Phasianidae
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:adel.html>adel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fazanten.html>fazanten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:genoten.html>genoten</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fazant.html>fazant</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:favoriete.html>favoriete</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:prooi.html>prooi</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jacht.html>jacht</a>, in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keuken.html>keuken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fazanten.html>fazanten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bereid.html>bereid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:prachtig.html>prachtig</a> pluimwild of <a href = vnd.unilang:verwerkt.html>verwerkt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:pastei.html>pastei</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:terwijl.html>terwijl</a> fazantenveren <a href = vnd.unilang:dames.html>dames</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heren.html>heren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tooien.html>tooien</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><i>The aristocracy always enjoyed <b>pheasants</b>: the <b>pheasant</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a favorite hunting prey, in the kitchen <b>pheasants</b> are prepared as splendid fowl or used in pie, while pheasant <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a> decorate <a href = vnd.unilang:ladies.html>ladies</a> and gentleman.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>The common pheasant, <i>Phasianus colchicus</i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gewone.html>gewone</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fazant.html>fazant</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:februari.html>februari</a> (6909)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">februārius</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:februari.html>februari</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>February</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
